import csv
import requests
from parsel import Selector

with open('链家.csv', mode='w', encoding='UTF-8', newline='') as f:
    csv_writer = csv.writer(f)
    csv_writer.writerow(['Direction', 'Area', 'Region', 'Price', 'URL'])

    for page in range(1, 101):
        url = f'https://bj.lianjia.com/zufang/pg{page}'
        headers = {
            'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/95.0.4638.54 Safari/537.36 Edg/95.0.1020.30'
        }
        response = requests.get(url=url, headers=headers)
        html_data = response.text
        selector = Selector(html_data)
        lis = selector.xpath('//div[@class="content__list"]/div')

        for li in lis:
            detail_buy = li.xpath('.//div/p/a/text()').get()
            detail_buy = detail_hire.strip()[0:2] if detail_hire else ''
            detail_url = 'https://bj.lianjia.com' + li.xpath('.//a/@href').get()
            detail_area = li.xpath('.//div/p[2]/text()[5]').get().strip() if li.xpath('.//div/p[2]/text()[5]') else ''
            detail_direction = li.xpath('.//div/p[2]/text()[6]').get().strip() if li.xpath('.//div/p[2]/text()[6]') else ''
            detail_houseinfo = li.xpath('.//div/p[2]/a[2]/text()').get() if li.xpath('.//div/p[2]/a[2]/text()') else ''
            detail_price = li.xpath('.//div/span/em/text()').get() if li.xpath('.//div/span/em/text()') else ''

            csv_writer.writerow([detail_houseinfo, detail_area, detail_direction, detail_price, detail_url])
            print(detail_houseinfo, detail_area, detail_direction, detail_price, detail_url, sep=' | ')

print("数据已成功爬取并保存为CSV文件。")
